## CSS Flexbox

### What is Flexbox?

Flexbox is a CSS box model to easily **layout**, **align** and **distribute** space among items within a **container** either horizontally or vertically.

‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé ‡¶´‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ CSS Box Model ‡¶Ø‡ßá Horizontally ‡¶¨‡¶æ Vertically ‡¶ï‡¶§‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ITEMS ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá Layout ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü, Align ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá Space Distribute ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

### CSS Flexbox Layout Module

Before the Flexbox Layout module, there were four layout modes:

1. Block, for sections in a webpage.
2. Inline, for text.
3. Table, for two-dimensional table data.
4. Positioned, for explicit position of an element.

**Note:** The Flexible Box Layout Module, makes it easier to design flexible responsive layout structure without using float or positioning.

### Flexbox Elements

- To start using the Flexbox model, you need to first define a flex container. ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé Flexbox Model ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Flex Container ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§
- ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Flex Model ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶á ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Flex Container ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé Flex Items ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Parent Element ( ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá Flex Container‡¶ì ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá) ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶ì‡¶á Flex Container/Parent Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ **_display_** property ‡¶è‡¶∞ Value **_flex_** ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
- Flex Container ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Direct Child ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Automatically **_Flex items_** ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Flex Container ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶É

![Flex Container](./chapter-13-css-flexbox/images/flex-container.png)

‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá Flex Container ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã Blue Area Element. ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶ü‡¶ø Flex Items ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã 1, 2 ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç 3.

Example: [Open in CodePen](https://codepen.io/CodeJogot/pen/WNaaXwJ)

#### Tips

- Using **_rem_** is good practice than using **_px_**.
- Using **_float_** is deprecated in modern programming. Use **_flexbox_** instead.

### Flex Direction

`flex-direction` ‡¶è‡¶∞ Value, by default ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá `row`. `flex-direction` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßü‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶É

- `flex-direction: row;`
- `flex-direction: row-reverse;`
- `flex-direction: column;`
- `flex-direction: column-reverse;`

`flex-wrap` has the following values:

- `flex-wrap: wrap;`
- `flex-wrap: no-wrap;`
- `flex-wrap: wrap-reverse;`

**Note:** The `flex-flow` property is a shorthand property for setting both the `flex-direction` and `flex-wrap` properties. Example: `flex-flow: row wrap;`

### Flex Direction Example

[Open Live Project in CodePen](https://codepen.io/CodeJogot/pen/XWxxzMv)

### Justify Content Property in Flex

- The `justify-content: center;` flex items ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá Container ‡¶è‡¶∞ Horizontally Center ‡¶è ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§
- The `justify-content: flex-start;` flex items ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá Container ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü (this is default).
- The `justify-content: flex-end;` flex items ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá Container ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü ‡•§
- The `justify-content: space-around;` flex items ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶ì ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® Space ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ Horizontally ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ù‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßá ‡•§
- The `justify-content: space-between;` flex items ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ù‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® Space ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ Horizontally ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ù‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßá ‡•§

![center](./chapter-13-css-flexbox/images/center.png)
![flex start](./chapter-13-css-flexbox/images/flex-start.png)
![flex end](./chapter-13-css-flexbox/images/flex-end.png)
![space around](./chapter-13-css-flexbox/images/space-around.png)
![space between](./chapter-13-css-flexbox/images/space-between.png)

### JUSTIFY CONTENT Property in Flex Example

[Open Live Project in CodePen](https://codepen.io/CodeJogot/pen/wvYYPem)

### ALIGN ITEMS Property in Flex

The align-items property is used to align the flex items.

- `align-items: center;` flex items ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá Vertically Center ‡¶è ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§
- `align-items: flex-start;` flex items ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá Vertically Top ‡¶è ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§
- `align-items: flex-end;` flex items ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá Vertically Bottom ‡¶è ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§
- `align-items: stretch;` stretches the flex items to fill the container (this is default).
- `align-items: baseline;` aligns the flex items such as their baselines aligns.

![align-items: center](./chapter-13-css-flexbox/images/align-center.png)
![align-items: flex start](./chapter-13-css-flexbox/images/align-flex-start.png)
![align-items: flex end](./chapter-13-css-flexbox/images/align-flex-end.png)
![align-items: baseline](./chapter-13-css-flexbox/images/align-baseline.png)

### ALIGN ITEMS Property in Flex Example

### The CSS Flexbox Container Properties Summary

|  **Property**   |                                                                                                                                                                          **Description**                                                                                                                                                                          |
| :-------------: | :---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------: |
|  align-content  | ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ `align-items` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã `align-items` ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶≤‡ßá Space ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶æ items ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶õ‡ßú‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá items ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá Vertically Align ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá `align-content` ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ ‡¶ì ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ item ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ì ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá space ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü, ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶ø items ‡¶ï‡ßá space ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶á vertically align ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ [align-content vs align-items Example](#align-content-vs-align-items-example) |
|   align-items   |                                                                                                                                                                Vertically Items ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá Align ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§                                                                                                                                                                 |
|     display     |                                                                                                                                                              Element ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶ø Type ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∂ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§                                                                                                                                                              |
| flex-direction  |                                                                                                            ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø Flex Container ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ Flex Container ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá Items ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ direction ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∂ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§                                                                                                            |
|    flex-flow    |                                                                                                                                                 ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø `flex-direction` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `flex-wrap` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø shorthand property.                                                                                                                                                  |
|    flex-wrap    |                                                                                                                                          Flex Items ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã wrap ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ, ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§                                                                                                                                          |
| justify-content |                                                                                                                     `align-items` ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã Vertically items ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá align ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá `justify-content` ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã Horizontally items ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá align ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§                                                                                                                      |

### ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ Flex Items Property

**_1. order_**

- `order` ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Flex Item Property, ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ Flex Items ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá, Flex Container ‡¶è ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§
- `oder` Property ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Markup Change ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶á, Flex items ‡¶è‡¶∞ order ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§

**_2. flex-grow_**

- `flex-grow` ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Flex Item Property, ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ Flex Items ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá, Flex Container ‡¶è ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§

- `flex-grow: 1` ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶§‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã Items ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶≤‡ßá Vertically or Horizontally ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ü‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßÅ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡¶ó‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá Resposive ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã behave ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé Browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡¶ó‡¶æ ‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ì ‡¶ß‡ßÄ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ß‡ßÄ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá, Browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡¶ó‡¶æ ‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ì ‡¶ß‡ßÄ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ß‡ßÄ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßú ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø Items ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ Fixed Width ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶á, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶ì ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Window Size ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡ßÄ Grow ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá ‡•§

**_3. flex-shrink_**

- `flex-shrink` `flex-grow` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ ‡¶â‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶Ø‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶®‡¶á `flex-grow: 1` ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® `flex-shrink` ‡¶è‡¶∞ Value‡¶ì 1 ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá Responsive ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§

**_4. flex-basis_**

- ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶á ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Flex Items ‡¶è‡¶∞ Width set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ min-width ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ min-width ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã, ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Item ‡¶è‡¶∞ `flex-basis: 200px` ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡¶ó‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá ‡¶ß‡ßÄ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ß‡ßÄ‡¶∞‡ßá Window Size ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡ßÄ ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ `min-width` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ñ‡¶®‡¶á ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á Responsive ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø `flex-basis` ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶á ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Property.

**_5. flex_**

- `flex` property ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã `flex-grow`, `flex-shrink` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `flex-basis` ‡¶è‡¶∞ shorthand property. ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®, `flex: 1 1 200px;`

## CSS Selectors

### What is CSS Selectors?

A CSS selector selects the HTML element(s) you want to style.

### Types of CSS Selectors

CSS Selectors ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡ß´ ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó‡ßá ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡¶É

1. Simple selectors (select elements based on name, id, class).
2. Combinator selectors (select elements based on a specific relationship between them).
3. Pseudo-class selectors (select elements based on a certain state).
4. Pseudo-elements selectors (select and style a part of an element).
5. Attribute selectors (select elements based on an attribute or attribute value).

### 01. Simple Selectors

CONTENTS WILL BE WRITTEN SOON INSHALLAH...

### 02: Combinator Selectors

A combinator is something that explains the relationship between the selectors.
A CSS selector can contain more than one simple selector. Between the simple selectors, we can include a combinator.
‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé, ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Selector ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï Simple Selectors ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á Simple Selectors ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá Combinator ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá Connect ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§

There are four different combinators in CSS:

1. Descendant selector (space)
2. Child selector (>)
3. Adjacent sibling selector (+)
4. General sibling selector (~)

#### Descendant Selector (Space)

Descendant Selector ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Under ‡¶è ‡¶Ø‡¶§ Child Elements ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ Select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á Child ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø Child ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶ì Select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®,

```css
div p {
  background-color: yellow;
}
```

‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá div element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶§ p element ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶¨ select ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

#### Child selector (>)

Child Selector ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ Immediate Child ‡¶ï‡ßá Select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Child ‡¶è‡¶∞ Child ‡¶ï‡ßá Select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ Descendant Select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

```css
div p {
  background-color: yellow;
}
```

‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá div element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Immediate Child Select ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé p select ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶á p ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ì ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì p ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã select ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§

#### Adjacent Sibling Selector (+)

‡¶è‡¶á Select ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶á ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé Adjacent Sibling Selector ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ Sibling ‡¶ï‡ßá Select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∂‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶¨‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶∏‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ö‡ßá‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá Select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®,

```html
<div>
  <p>Paragraph 1 in the div.</p>
  <p>Paragraph 2 in the div.</p>
</div>

<p>Paragraph 3. After a div.</p>
<p>Paragraph 4. After a div.</p>

<div>
  <p>Paragraph 5 in the div.</p>
  <p>Paragraph 6 in the div.</p>
</div>

<p>Paragraph 7. After a div.</p>
<p>Paragraph 8. After a div.</p>
```

```css
div + p {
  background-color: yellow;
}
```

‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `<p>Paragraph 3. After a div.</p>` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `<p>Paragraph 7. After a div.</p>` ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡ßã Selector Select ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

#### General Sibling Selector (~)

General sibling selector (~) ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶¨ ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶¨‡ßã‡¶®‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶á Select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®,

```html
<div>
  <p>Paragraph 1 in the div.</p>
  <p>Paragraph 2 in the div.</p>
</div>

<p>Paragraph 3. After a div.</p>
<p>Paragraph 4. After a div.</p>

<div>
  <p>Paragraph 5 in the div.</p>
  <p>Paragraph 6 in the div.</p>
</div>

<p>Paragraph 7. After a div.</p>
<p>Paragraph 8. After a div.</p>
```

```css
div + p {
  background-color: yellow;
}
```

‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `<p>Paragraph 3. After a div.</p>` , `<p>Paragraph 4. After a div.</p>` , `<p>Paragraph 7. After a div.</p>` , `<p>Paragraph 8. After a div.</p>` ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶¨‡ßã‡¶® Select ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

### 03. Pseudo-class Selectors

Pseudo-class Selector ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® State ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®, ‡¶è‡¶á Selector ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡¶É
‡ßß‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶∏ ‡¶π‡ßã‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü,
‡ß®‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Link Visit ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶Ç‡¶¨‡¶æ Univisted ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü,
‡ß©‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Element ‡¶ï‡ßá Focus ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§

#### Syntax

```css
selector:pseudo-class {
  property: value;
}
```

#### Anchor Pseudo-classes

Example:

```css
/* unvisited link */
a:link {
  color: #ff0000;
}

/* visited link */
a:visited {
  color: #00ff00;
}

/* mouse over link */
a:hover {
  color: #ff00ff;
}

/* selected link */
a:active {
  color: #0000ff;
}
```

**Note:** `a:hover` MUST come after `a:link` and `a:visited` in the CSS definition in order to be effective! `a:active` MUST come after `a:hover` in the CSS definition in order to be effective! Pseudo-class names are not case-sensitive.

#### Pseudo-classes and HTML Classes

Pseudo-classes can be combined with HTML classes:
When you hover over the link in the example, it will change color:

```css
a.highlight:hover {
  color: #ff0000;
}
```

#### Hover on `<div>`

‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Div Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ Hover ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶ê Div Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§
‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®,

```css
div {
  background-color: green;
  color: white;
  padding: 25px;
  text-align: center;
}

div:hover {
  background-color: blue;
}
```

#### Simple Tooltip Hover

Hover over a <div> element to show a <p> element (like a tooltip):
Example:

```html
<div class="simple-class-hover">
  Hover me this DIV element to show the P element.
  <p class="tool-tip">Tada! I'm here!</p>
</div>
```

```css
.tool-tip {
  display: none;
  background-color: coral;
}

.simple-class-hover:hover p {
  display: block;
}
```

#### CSS - The ':first-child' Pseudo-class

‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø `p:first-child` ‡¶è‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶Å‡ßú‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá p ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶∏‡¶¨ Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ Child Element ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶ê‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶æ Select ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®,

```html
<div>
  <p>This is Paragraph 1</p>
  <p>This is Paragraph 2</p>
  <p>This is Paragraph 3</p>
</div>
<div>
  <p>This is Paragraph 4</p>
  <p>This is Paragraph 5</p>
  <p>This is Paragraph 6</p>
</div>
```

```css
p:first-child {
  background-color: bisque;
}
```

‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá Paragraph 1 ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Paragraph 4 Select ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

#### Match The First `<i>` Element in All `<p>` Elements

‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø `i:first-child` ‡¶è‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶á, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶ê‡¶∏‡¶¨ i element select ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ child element. ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø `p i:first-child` ‡¶è‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶á, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶∏‡¶¨ p element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ child i element ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶ê‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã select ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

Example:

```html
<p>This is <i>1st</i> i element. This is <i>2nd</i> i element.</p>
<p>This is <i>3rd</i> i element. This is <i>4th</i> i element.</p>
<div>This is <i>5th</i> i element. This is <i>6th</i> i element.</div>
```

```css
p i:first-child {
  background-color: red;
}
```

‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶≤‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®, Div Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ i element ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ Select ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶á‡•§

#### Match all `<i>` elements in all first child `<p>` elements

`p:first-child i` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã, ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ P element ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® element ‡¶è‡¶∞ first child ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶ê p element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶§ i element ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶¨ i elements ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá ‡•§

Example:

```html
<body>
  <h1>Match all i elements in all first child p elements</h1>
  <div>
    <p>This is <i>1st</i> paragraph. <i>This is another i element</i></p>
    <p>This is <i>2nd</i> paragraph <i>This is another i element</i></p>
  </div>
  <article>
    <p>This is <i>3rd</i> paragraph <i>This is another i element</i></p>
    <p>This is <i>4th</i> paragraph <i>This is another i element</i></p>
  </article>
  <article>
    <p>
      <i>1</i>
      <i>2</i>
      <i>3</i>
    </p>
    <p>
      <i>4</i>
      <i>5</i>
      <i>6</i>
    </p>
  </article>
</body>
```

```css
p:first-child i {
  color: red;
}
```

### All CSS Pseudo Classes

| Selector No. | Selector Name        | Example               | Example Description                                                                                      |
| ------------ | -------------------- | --------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| 01           | :root                | root                  | Selects the document's root element                                                                      |
| 02           | :link                | a:link                | Selects all unvisited links                                                                              |
| 03           | :visited             | a:visited             | Selects all visited links                                                                                |
| 04           | :hover               | a:hover               | Selects links on mouse over                                                                              |
| 05           | :active              | a:active              | Selects the active link.                                                                                 |
| 06           | :target              | #news:target          | Selects the current active #news element (clicked on a URL containing that anchor name)                  |
| 07           | :checked             | input:checked         | Selects every checked `<input>` element                                                                  |
| 08           | :enabled             | input:enabled         | Selects every enabled `<input>` element                                                                  |
| 09           | :disabled            | input:disabled        | Selects every disabled `<input>` element                                                                 |
| 10           | :focus               | input:focus           | Selects the `<input>` element that has focus                                                             |
| 11           | :in-range            | input:in-range        | Selects `<input>` elements with a value within a specified range                                         |
| 12           | :out-of-range        | input:out-of-range    | Selects `<input>` elements with a value outside a specified range                                        |
| 13           | :valid               | input:valid           | Selects all `<input>` elements with a valid value                                                        |
| 14           | :invalid             | input:invalid         | Selects all `<input>` elements with an invalid value                                                     |
| 15           | :optional            | input:optional        | Selects `<input>` elements with no "required" attribute                                                  |
| 16           | :required            | input:required        | Selects `<input>` elements with a "required" attribute specified                                         |
| 17           | :read-only           | input:read-only       | Selects `<input>` elements with a "readonly" attribute specified                                         |
| 18           | :read-write          | input:read-write      | Selects `<input>` elements with no "readonly" attribute                                                  |
| 19           | :empty               | p:empty               | Selects every `<p>` element that has no children                                                         |
| 20           | :first-child         | p:first-child         | Selects every `<p>` elements that is the first child of its parent                                       |
| 21           | :last-child          | p:last-child          | Selects every `<p>` elements that is the last child of its parent                                        |
| 22           | :first-of-type       | p:first-of-type       | Selects every `<p>` element that is the first `<p>` element of its parent                                |
| 23           | :last-of-type        | p:last-of-type        | Selects every `<p>` element that is the last `<p>` element of its parent                                 |
| 24           | :lang(language)      | p:lang(it)            | Selects every `<p>` element with a lang attribute value starting with "it"                               |
| 25           | :not(selector)       | :not(p)               | Selects every element that is not a `<p>` element                                                        |
| 26           | :nth-child(n)        | p:nth-child(2)        | Selects every `<p>` element that is the second child of its parent                                       |
| 27           | :nth-last-child(n)   | p:nth-last-child(2)   | Selects every `<p>` element that is the second child of its parent, counting from the last child         |
| 28           | :nth-of-type(n)      | p:nth-of-type(2)      | Selects every `<p>` element that is the second `<p>` element of its parent                               |
| 29           | :nth-last-of-type(n) | p:nth-last-of-type(2) | Selects every `<p>` element that is the second `<p>` element of its parent, counting from the last child |
| 30           | :only-of-type        | p:only-of-type        | Selects every `<p>` element that is the only `<p>` element of its parent                                 |
| 31           | :only-child          | p:only-child          | Selects every `<p>` element that is the only child of its parent                                         |

#### `:target` Pseudo-class

`:target` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã, ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Anchor Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ href Attribute ‡¶è ‡¶Ø‡ßá Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Id ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á Element ‡¶ï‡ßá Select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

Example:

```html
<body>
  <h1>`:target` Pseudo-class</h1>
  <div>
    <a href="#article-01">Go To Article 01</a>
  </div>
  <div>
    <a href="#article-02">Go To Article 02</a>
  </div>
  <article>
    <h2 id="article-01">Article-01</h2>
    Codejogot is an programming platform. It helps the students learn with fun.
    Codejogot is an programming platform. It helps the students learn with fun.
  </article>
  <article>
    <h2 id="article-02">Article-02</h2>
    During my university life, I used to solve competitive programming problems
    in various online judges such as UVa, CodeForces, TopCoder, HackerRank,
    GeeksforGeeks etc. Till now, I've solved more than 1300 problems in these
    sites. Now-a-days, I spend most of the time in farming, travelling and
    developing my own projects and ideas.
  </article>
</body>
```

```css
:target {
  border: 2px solid darkorange;
  background-color: bisque;
}
```

![target](./chapter-14-css-selectors/images/2.png)

#### Pseudo-class `:checked`

‡¶Ø‡ßá `input` element ‡¶è `checked` attribute ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ê element ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ element ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶∞ width and height ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

Example:

```html
<body>
  <h1>Psedo-class `:checked`</h1>
  <form action="">
    <input type="radio" checked="checked" />
    <label for="">Male</label> <br />
    <input type="radio" />
    <label for="">Female</label> <br />
    <input type="checkbox" checked="checked" />
    <label for="">C++</label> <br />
    <input type="checkbox" />
    <label for="">Python</label>
  </form>
</body>
```

```css
input:checked {
  height: 20px;
  width: 20px;
}
```

#### Pseudo-class `:enabled` and `:disabled`

`:enabled` ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á Input Elements ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ Select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ property `disabled` ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶á‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá `:disabled` ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á Input Elements ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ Select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ property `disabled` ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

Example:

```html
<body>
  <h1>`:enabled` and `:disabled` Pseudo-class</h1>
  <form action="">
    <label for="">First Name</label>
    <input type="text" /> <br />
    <label for="">Last Name</label>
    <input type="text" /> <br />
    <label for="">Country</label>
    <input type="text" disabled value="Bangladesh" /> <br />
  </form>
</body>
```

```css
input[type="text"]:enabled {
  background-color: darkgray;
}

input[type="text"]:disabled {
  background-color: red;
}
```

#### `:focus` Pseudo-class

‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Input Element ‡¶è ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® Click ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Mouse ‡¶è‡¶∞ Cursor ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® `:focus` Selector ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ê Input Element ‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá Select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

```html
<form action="">
  <label for="">Name</label>
  <input type="text" /> <br />
```

#### `:in-range` and `:out-of-range` Pseudo-class

‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Input Field ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡ßá Value ‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø Range ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá `:in-range` Selector ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßü `:out-of-range` ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

Example:

```html
<input type="number" min="5" max="10" value="7" />
```

```css
input:in-range {
  background-color: green;
  color: white;
}

input:out-of-range {
  background-color: red;
  color: white;
}
```

#### Read-only and Read-write Pseudo-class

‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Input Element ‡¶è ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø `readonly` attribute ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá `:read-only` Pseudo-class ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßü, `read-write` Pseudo-class ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

#### First-child and Last-child Pseudo-class

‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø `p:first-child` ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® p ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® element ‡¶è‡¶∞ first child ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶ê p ‡¶ï‡ßá select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø `p:last-child` ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® p ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® element ‡¶è‡¶∞ last child ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶ê p ‡¶ï‡ßá select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

Example:

```html
<div>
  <p>This is Paragraph 1</p>
  <p>This is Paragraph 2</p>
  <p>This is Paragraph 3</p>
</div>
<article>
  <p>This is Paragraph 4</p>
  <p>This is Paragraph 5</p>
  <p>This is Paragraph 6</p>
</article>
<p>This is Paragraph 7</p>
```

```css
p:first-child {
  background-color: greenyellow;
}
p:last-child {
  background-color: yellow;
}
```

#### First-of-type and Last-of-type Pseudo-class

`p:first-of-type` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Parent Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã child elements ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ ‡¶Ø‡ßá p element ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶®‡ßü ‡¶Ø‡ßá, ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ child ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá, `p:last-of-type` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Parent Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã child elements ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶Ø‡ßá p element ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

Example:

```html
<body>
  <h1>First-of-type and Last-of-type Pseudo-class</h1>
  <p>this is paragraph 1</p>
  <p>this is paragraph 2</p>
  <h3>this is h3</h3>
  <div>
    <h4>this is h4</h4>
    <p>this is paragraph 4</p>
    <p>this is paragraph 5</p>
    <h3>this is another h3</h3>
  </div>
</body>
```

```css
p:first-of-type {
  background-color: greenyellow;
}
p:last-of-type {
  background-color: burlywood;
}
```

Screenshot:

![first-of-type](./chapter-14-css-selectors/images/12.png)

[Open in CodePen](https://codepen.io/travelerabdulalim/pen/xxjLYyP)

#### :not Pseudo-class

`:not(p)` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã, p elements ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶¨ elements ‡¶ï‡ßá select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

Example:

```html
<body>
  <h1>:not() Pseudo-class</h1>
  <p>this is paragraph 1</p>
  <p>this is paragraph 2</p>
  <div>this is a div element</div>
</body>
```

```css
p {
  color: black;
}

:not(p) {
  color: darkorange;
}
```

Screenshot:

![not](./chapter-14-css-selectors/images/13.png)

#### :nth-child() Pseudo-class

`p:nth-child(2)` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Parent Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ 2 ‡¶®‡¶Ç Child Element ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø p ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶ê p ‡¶ï‡ßá select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

Example:

```html
<body>
  <h1>nth-child() Pseudo-class</h1>
  <div>
    <h4>this is h4</h4>
    <p>This is Paragraph 1</p>
    <p>This is Paragraph 2</p>
  </div>
  <div>
    <h4>this is another h4</h4>
    <p>This is Paragraph 5</p>
    <p>This is Paragraph 6</p>
  </div>
</body>
```

```css
p:nth-child(2) {
  color: red;
}
```

#### nth-last-child() Pseudo-class

‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø nth-child() ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶á, nth-child() ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü Count ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ nth-last-child() ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá count ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§

Example:

```html
<body>
  <h1>nth-last-child() Pseudo-class</h1>
  <div>
    <p>This is Paragraph 1</p>
    <p>This is Paragraph 2</p>
    <h4>this is h4</h4>
  </div>
  <div>
    <p>This is Paragraph 5</p>
    <p>This is Paragraph 6</p>
    <h4>this is another h4</h4>
  </div>
</body>
```

```css
p:nth-last-child(2) {
  color: red;
}
```

#### nth-of-type() Pseudo-class

`p:nth-of-type(2)` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Parent Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ 2 ‡¶®‡¶Ç p element ‡¶ï‡ßá select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

‡¶Ü‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ ‡¶â‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶á, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®, `:nth-of-type(2)` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã Parent Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ 2 ‡¶®‡¶Ç Child Element ‡¶ï‡ßá select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

Example:

```html
<body>
  <h1>nth-of-type Pseudo-class</h1>
  <div>
    <p>This is some text.</p>
  </div>
  <div>
    <p>This is some text.</p>
  </div>
  <div>
    <p>This is some text.</p>
  </div>
  <ul>
    <li>First list item</li>
    <li>Second list item</li>
    <li>Third list item</li>
    <li>Fourth list item</li>
    <li>Fifth list item</li>
  </ul>
</body>
```

```css
div:nth-of-type(2) {
  color: red;
}
li:nth-of-type(2) {
  color: lightgreen;
}

:nth-of-type(3) {
  color: blue;
}
```

#### nth-of-last-type()

‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø `:nth-of-type` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶á, ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá count ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

#### only-of-type Pseudo-class

`p:only-of-type` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶∏‡¶ï‡¶≤ Parent Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Child ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ p, ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á p ‡¶ï‡ßá select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Parent Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï p ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§

Example:

```html
<body>
  <h1>only-of-type</h1>
  <div>
    <p>This is Paragraph 1</p>
  </div>
  <div>
    <p>This is Paragraph 2</p>
    <p>This is Paragraph 3</p>
  </div>
</body>
```

```css
p:only-of-type {
  background-color: lightgreen;
}
```

`p:only-child` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Parent Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø p element ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá ‡•§

Example:

```html
<body>
  <h1>Only-child Pseudo-class</h1>
```

```css
p:only-child {
```

### 04. All CSS Pseudo Elements

**Pseudo Element ‡¶ï‡¶ø**

Pseudo Element ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Keyword ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Selector ‡¶è‡¶∞ Specific ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶ï‡ßá Style ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Element ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶õ‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ‡¶á‡•§ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡ßá Specific ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶ï‡ßá Style ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡¶ø, ‡¶ê ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá Style ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶§, ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Element ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶ó‡¶§‡ßã‡•§ Pseudo Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Element ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶õ‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶ê Specific ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Style ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®‡¶É ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Paragraph ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶® ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ Letter ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Pseudo Element ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§

**Note:** ::before, ::after ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Element. ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé CSS ‡¶è Div, Span, Section ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® Element ‡¶§‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶ê‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶ì (::before, ::after, ::first-letter) ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Element. ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç by default ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã Inline Element.

| **Selector No.** | **Selector Name** |   **Example**   |                   **Example Description**                    |
| :--------------: | :---------------: | :-------------: | :----------------------------------------------------------: |
|        01        |      ::after      |    p::after     |              Insert content after `<p>` element              |
|        02        |     ::before      |    p::before    |             Insert content before `<p>` element              |
|        03        |  ::first-letter   | p::first-letter |          Selects the first letter of `<p>` element           |
|        04        |   ::first-line    |  p::first-line  |           Selects the first line of `<p>` element            |
|        05        |    ::selection    |  p::selection   | Selects the portion of an element that is selected by a user |

#### Example

```html
<body>
  <h1>Pseudo Elements</h1>
  <p>Abdul Alim</p>
  <p>Rafiqul Islam</p>
</body>
```

```css
p::before {
  content: "Name: ";
}

p::after {
  content: " Country: Bangladesh ";
}

p::first-letter {
  font-size: 5rem;
  color: pink;
}

p::first-line {
  background-color: lightcyan;
}

p::selection {
  background-color: red;
}
```

#### Screenshot

![pseudo-elements](./chapter-14-css-selectors/images/19.png)

#### Source Codes

[Open Project in CodePen](https://codepen.io/travelerabdulalim/pen/YzLxLJV)

#### Marker Pseudo Element

`::marker` Pseudo Element ‡¶ü‡¶ø list items coloring ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§

Example:

```html
<ul>
  <li>C++</li>
  <li>Java</li>
  <li>Python</li>
  <li>Kotlin</li>
</ul>
<ol>
  <li>Farmer</li>
  <li>Traveller</li>
  <li>Developer</li>
</ol>
```

```css
::marker {
  color: red;
}
```

Screenshot:

![marker](./chapter-14-css-selectors/images/20.png)

[Open in Codepen](https://codepen.io/travelerabdulalim/pen/abGyGXd)

### 05. Attribute Selectors

| Selector No. | Selector Name       | Example              | Example Description                                                                       |
| ------------ | ------------------- | -------------------- | ----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| 01           | [attribute]         | [target]             | Selects all elements with a target attribute                                              |
| 02           | [attribute=value]   | [target=_blank]      | Selects all elements with target="\_blank"                                                |
| 03           | [attribute~=value]  | [title~=flower]      | Selects all elements with a title attribute containing the word "flower"                  |
| 04           | [attribute\|=value] | [lang\|=en]          | Selects all elements with a lang attribute value starting with "en"                       |
| 05           | [attribute^=value]  | a[href^="https"]     | Selects every `<a>` element whose href attribute value begins with "https"                |
| 06           | [attribute$=value]  | a[href$=".pdf"]      | Selects every `<a>` element whose href attribute value ends with ".pdf"                   |
| 07           | [attribute*=value]  | a[href*="w3schools"] | Selects every `<a>` element whose href attribute value contains the substring "w3schools" |

Note: This table has some type because of vs-code extensions, plz visit https://www.w3schools.com/css/css_attribute_selectors.asp for original table.

#### Example Source Codes

```html
<body>
  <h1>Attribute Selectors</h1>
  <a href="http://google.com" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer"
    >Google</a
  >
  <a href="http://google.com">Google</a>
  <img
    src="/chapter-14-css-selectors/images/logo.png"
    title="Codejogot Logo"
    alt="CodeJogot"
    width="300px"
    height="300px"
  />
  <img
    src="/chapter-14-css-selectors/images/fb-cover.png"
    title=" at Dhaka"
    alt="CodeJogot"
    width="300px"
    height="300px"
  />
</body>
```

```css
a[target] {
  color: red;
}
/* attribute with value */
a[target="_blank"] {
  background-color: aquamarine;
}
/* title text anywhere */
img[title~="Logo"] {
  border: 2px solid red;
}
/* start with*/
a[href^="http"] {
  font-size: 2rem;
}
/* end with */
img[alt$="Jogot"] {
  border-radius: 50%;
}
/* substring */
a[href*="google"] {
  font-style: italic;
}
```

![attr](./chapter-14-css-selectors/images/21.png)

### Text Alignment & Text Direction Properties

| **Property Name** | **Property Values**                                              | **Role/Task**                                                          | **Example**                                                                                                         |
| ----------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `text-align`      | left, right, center, justify                                     | ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ü‡¶ï‡ßá Horizontally Align ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶á Property ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ | `text-align: center`. ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® element ‡¶è ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶ê Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ü ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ù‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§     |
| `text-align-last` | left, right, center, justify                                     | ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Text ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶®‡¶ï‡ßá Align ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§                    | `text-align-last: right` ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ P element ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶ê P element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶® ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá align ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ |
| `direction`       | ltr, rtl                                                         |                                                                        |                                                                                                                     |
| `unicode-bidi`    | normal, embed, bidi-override                                     |                                                                        |                                                                                                                     |
| `vertical-align`  | baseline, length, sub, super, top, text-top, middle, text-bottom | inline ‡¶¨‡¶æ inline-block or table-cell box ‡¶ï‡ßá Vertically Align ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá       |                                                                                                                     |

## CSS Links

- ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶Ç‡¶ï ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡ßü `<a>` ‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ó ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡•§ HTML ‡¶è ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶Ç‡¶ï ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá By Default ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ Styles Generate ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ CSS ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá Customize ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§

### Four States of Links

Link ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶æ States ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶æ Pseudo-class ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá CSS ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§

- `a:link` - a normal, unvisited link.
- `a:visited` - a link the user has visited.
- `a:hover` - a link when the user mouses over it.
- `a:active` - a link the moment it is clicked.

_Note: CSS ‡¶è Code ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶á link ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç visited Pseudo-class ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞ hover Pseudo-class ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç active hover ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§_

#### Example:

![links](./chapter-16/images/link.png)

#### Source Codes:

[Open in CodePen](https://codepen.io/CodeJogot/pen/XWyVZdP)

### How To Create Link Boxes/Buttons

```css
a:link,
a:visited {
  background-color: white;
  border: 2px solid black;
  text-decoration: none;
  color: black;
  padding: 8px 24px;
  text-align: center;
  border-radius: 4px;
}

a:hover,
a:active {
  background-color: black;
  color: white;
}
```

Example:

![link-box](./chapter-16/images/link-box.png)

Source Codes:
[Open in CodePen](https://codepen.io/CodeJogot/pen/ZEmvoQB)

- Ordered List Bullet ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§

- `list-style-position: outside` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ü ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü Items ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
- `list-style-position: inside` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ü ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü Items ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
- ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ü ‡¶™‡ßü‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Border ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶° ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨ ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§

### How to Remove Default Settings

- ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø, ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶®‡¶á ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ü ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ Default Margin Padding ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶° ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶Ç Remove ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶∞ Code ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶É

```css
ul {
  list-style-type: none;
  margin: 0;
  padding: 0;
}
```

- ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Website Layout ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßü‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ñ‡ßá‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã, ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡ßá Website ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶¨‡¶∞ (Row) ‡¶ï‡ßü‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó‡ßá ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü, ‡¶è‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ê ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö (row) ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Æ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶® (column) ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶¨‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßü‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó‡ßá ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á Sub-section ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶¨‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶æ, ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Æ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶¨‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶á‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶§‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã Website ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Website ‡¶è‡¶∞ Layout ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§

# Chapter-20: CSS Grid Layout

### A Sample Example of CSS Grid Layout Module

![CSS Grid Layout Module](./chapter-20-css-grid-layout/images/css-grid-layout.png)

### Basic Concept And Benefits of CSS Grid Layout

- The CSS Grid Layout Module offers a grid-based layout system, with rows and columns, making it easier to design web pages without having to use floats and positioning.
- CSS Grid Layout ‡¶è Multidimensional Layout ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá Row and Column ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá CSS Flexbox ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã One Dimensional, ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ Row ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ Column ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§
- Simpler Markup.
- Framework not needed. ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ Multi-dimensional Grid ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Framework ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶á, ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú CSS Grid ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨ ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶´‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§
- Great Browsers Support.
- CSS Grid ‡¶è‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßü CSS Flexbox ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶¨‡¶æ ! :D ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶® CSS Grid ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Flexbox ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶á, plus ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï Features ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßã, ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá 2-dimensional (row and column both) Scenario ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá CSS Grid ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨ ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶®‡•§

### Grid Elements

- A grid layout consists of a parent element (Grid Container), with one or more child elements. ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Grid Layout ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Parent Element ‡¶¨‡¶æ Grid Container ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá, Grid Container ‡¶è‡¶∞ Under ‡¶è ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï Grid Elements ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
- ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Grid Layout ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá Grid Container ‡¶è‡¶∞ CSS Property ‡¶§‡ßá `display: grid;` ‡¶Ö‡¶•‡¶¨‡¶æ `display: inline-grid` ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

### All CSS Grid Properties

|       **Property**        |                                         **Syntax**                                          |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      **Description**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| :-----------------------: | :-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------: | :------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------: |
|      **column-gap**       |                        column-gap: length\|normal\|initial\|inherit;                        |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   The column-gap property sets the gap between the columns. Example: `column-gap: 50px;`                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
|        **row-gap**        |                         row-gap: length\|normal\|initial\|inherit;                          |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       The row-gap property sets the gap between the rows. Example: `row-gap: 50px;`                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
|          **gap**          |                                  gap: row-gap column-gap;                                   |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     The gap property is a shorthand property for the row-gap and the column-gap properties. Example: `gap: 25px 50px;`                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
|  **gird-template-rows**   |     grid-template-rows: none\|auto\|max-content\|min-content\|length\|initial\|inherit;     |                                                                               The `grid-template-rows` property specifies the number and the heights of the rows in a grid layout. Example-01: `grid-template-rows: 50px 100px 70px 120px 150px;` Here, there are 5 rows. 1st row size is 50px, 2nd row size is 100px, 3rd row size is 70px, 4th row size is 120px and 5th row size is 150px. Example-02: `grid-template-rows: auto auto auto;`, means there are 3 rows with equal row size depending on the Grid Containers Height. Example-03: `grid-template-rows: 1fr 2fr 1fr;` , ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ Window ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡ß™ ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡ßß ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ Row ‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡ß® ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßÄ‡ßü Row ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡ßß ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßÉ‡¶§‡ßÄ‡ßü Row ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ 100% Responsive.                                                                                |
| **grid-template-columns** |   grid-template-columns: none\|auto\|max-content\|min-content\|length\|initial\|inherit;    |                                                              The `grid-template-columns` property specifies the number and the heights of the columns in a grid layout. Example-01: `grid-template-rows: 50px 100px 70px 120px 150px;` Here, there are 5 columns. 1st column size is 50px, 2nd column size is 100px, 3rd column size is 70px, 4th column size is 120px and 5th column size is 150px. Example-02: `grid-template-columns: auto auto auto;`, means there are 3 columns with equal column size depending on the Grid Containers Width. Example-03: `grid-template-columns: 3fr 2fr 3fr` , ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã Window ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡ßÆ ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó‡ßá ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡ß© ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ Column ‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡ß® ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßÄ‡ßü ‡¶ï‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡ß© ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßÉ‡¶§‡ßÄ‡ßü ‡¶ï‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ 100% Responsive.                                                               |
|    **grid-row-start**     |                           grid-row-start: auto\|row-line\|span n;                           | ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Grid Element ‡¶ï‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ Row-line ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶õ‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Grid Element ‡¶ï‡¶§‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã Row ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡¶ó‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶¶‡¶ñ‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ì ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶è‡¶á Property ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§ Example-01: `grid-row-start: auto;` ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ By default Property. ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé ‡¶Ø‡ßá Grid Element ‡¶è‡¶á Property set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßã‡¶ï ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶®, ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ Grid Element ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶á Grid Render ‡¶π‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Example-02: `grid-row-start: span 3;` , ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø 2 ‡¶®‡¶Ç Grid Element ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá 2 ‡¶®‡¶Ç Grid Element ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶ü‡¶æ Row ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡¶ó‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡¶ñ‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Example-03: `grid-row-start: 2;` ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø 3 ‡¶®‡¶Ç Grid Element ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá 3 ‡¶®‡¶Ç Grid Element 2 ‡¶®‡¶Ç Row-line ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßü‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶∞ W3 Schools ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ô‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡•§ https://www.w3schools.com/cssref/playdemo.asp?filename=playcss_grid-row-start |
|     **grid-row-end**      |                            grid-row-end: auto\|row-line\|span n;                            |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           Example-01: `grid-row-end: 3;` , ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø 2 ‡¶®‡¶Ç Grid Element ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá 2 ‡¶®‡¶Ç Grid Element 3 ‡¶®‡¶Ç Row-line ‡¶è End ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã Practice and Visualize ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ô‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶É https://www.w3schools.com/cssref/playdemo.asp?filename=playcss_grid-row-end                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
|   **grid-column-start**   |                        grid-column-start: auto\|span n\|column-line;                        |                                                                                                                                                                                            The grid-column-start property defines on which column-line the item will start. Example-01: `grid-column-start: 3;`, ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡ß® ‡¶®‡¶Ç ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶° ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶° ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡ß© ‡¶®‡¶Ç Column-line ‡¶è ‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡ß® ‡¶®‡¶Ç ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶° ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶õ‡¶ø‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá? ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Å‡¶ï‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ô‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßÅ‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡ßã : https://www.w3schools.com/cssref/playdemo.asp?filename=playcss_grid-column-start                                                                                                                                                                                            |
|    **grid-column-end**    |                         grid-column-end: auto\|span n\|column-line;                         |                                                                                                                                                                                                          The grid-column-end property defines how many columns an item will span, or on which column-line the item will end. Example-01: `grid-column-end: 3;` ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡ßß ‡¶®‡¶Ç ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶° ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡ßß ‡¶®‡¶Ç ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶° ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡ß© ‡¶®‡¶Ç Column-line ‡¶è End ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶Ç‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßá Visualize ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡ßã‡¶É https://www.w3schools.com/cssref/playdemo.asp?filename=playcss_grid-column-end&preval=5                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
|       **grid-row**        |                          grid-row: grid-row-start / grid-row-end;                           |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         Example-01: `grid-row: 1 / 3`, ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé ‡¶Ø‡ßá Element ‡¶è ‡¶è‡¶á Property ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á Element ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡ßß ‡¶®‡¶Ç row-line ‡¶è ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡ß© ‡¶®‡¶Ç row-line ‡¶è ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |
|      **grid-column**      |                      grid-column: grid-column-start / grid-column-end;                      |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    Example-01: `grid-column: 1 / 3`, ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé ‡¶Ø‡ßá Element ‡¶è ‡¶è‡¶á Property ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á Element ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡ßß ‡¶®‡¶Ç column-line ‡¶è ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡ß© ‡¶®‡¶Ç column-line ‡¶è ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
|       **grid-area**       | grid-area: grid-row-start / grid-column-start / grid-row-end / grid-column-end \| itemname; |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                Example-01: `grid-area: h;`                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
|  **grid-template-areas**  |                            grid-template-areas: none\|itemnames;                            |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     Example-01: `grid-template-areas: "m h h h h h h h h h h h" "m c c c c c c c c c c c" "f f f f f f f f f f f f";`                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
|    **justify-content**    |       justify-content: start\|end\|center\|space-between\|space-around\|space-evenly;       |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               Example-01: `justify-content: center;` ‡¶è‡¶á Property ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Container ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶ê Container ‡¶è ‡¶Ø‡¶§‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã Items ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶¨ Horizontally Center ‡¶è ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
|     **align-content**     |        align-content: start\|end\|center\|space-between\|space-around\|space-evenly;        |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 Example-01: `align-content: center;` ‡¶è‡¶á Property ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Container ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶ê Container ‡¶è ‡¶Ø‡¶§‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã Items ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶¨ Vertically Center ‡¶è ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |

### CSS Grid Tips

- Shorthand property of `grid-template-rows` and `grid-template-columns` is `grid-template: `grid-template-rows / grid-template-columns`.
- ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ `grid-template-rows: 1fr 1fr 1fr 1fr 1fr` ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡ß´ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶™‡ßá `grid-template-rows: repeat(5, 1fr)` ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§

## CSS Gradients Introduction

### Basic Concepts of CSS Gradients

- CSS gradients let you display smooth transitions between two or more specified colors.

### Types of Gradients

1. Linear Gradients (goes down/up/left/right/diagonally).
2. Radial Gradients (defined by their center).
3. Conic Gradients (rotated around a center point).

## Linear Gradients

- Linear Gradients ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶§ ‡ß® ‡¶ü‡¶ø Colors ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶ó‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶ø, `background-image: linear-gradient(red, blue);` ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶∞‡¶Ç ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡ßÄ‡¶≤ ‡¶∞‡¶Ç Transition ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶¨‡¶∞ (Top to Bottom), ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ By default ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø, ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á By default ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§

### Syntax of Linear Gradients

`background-image: linear-gradient(direction, color-stop1, color-stop2, ...);`

### Direction of Linear Gradients

- Linear Gradient ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Color ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ß‡ßÄ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ß‡ßÄ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Color ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶á‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá Transition ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Color ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶•‡¶æ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶ó‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßÄ‡ßü Color ‡¶è Transition ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ `Direction` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§

### Direction - Top to Bottom (this is default )

- ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Direction ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶á, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá by default, Top to Bottom ‡¶è Transition ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡ßá Color sets ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶¨‡ßã ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ by default ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá Transition ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

Example: `background-image: linear-gradients(red, yellow);` . This linear gradient starts red, transitioning to yellow.

Output Screenshot:

![Top to Bottom](./chapter-21-css-gradients/images/to-to-bottom.png)

### Direction - Left to Right

Example: `background-image: linear-gradients(to right, red, yellow);`
The following example shows a linear gradient that starts from the left. It starts red, transitioning to yellow.

Output Screenshot:

![Left to Right](./chapter-21-css-gradients/images/left-to-right.png)

### Direction - Top Left to Bottom Right

Example: `background-image: linear-gradients( to bottom right, red, yellow);`
The following example shows a linear gradient that starts at top left (and goes to bottom right). It starts red, transitioning to yellow.

Output Screenshot:

![Topleft to Bottomright](./chapter-21-css-gradients/images/topleft-to-bottomright.png)

### Direction - 180deg

‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø Direction ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø Control ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡ßá Pre-defined Directions (to bottom, to top, to right, to left, to bottom right, etc.) ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶¶‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Angle ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ A value of 0deg is equivalent to "to top". A value of 90deg is equivalent to "to right". A value of 180deg is equivalent to "to bottom".
‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶π‡ßá‡¶§‡ßÅ `to bottom` ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã by default property, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á `180deg` ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá by default property. ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ ‡¶ì ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßÄ‡ßü Color ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Line ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü, ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á Line ‡¶≠‡ßÇ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá 180 Degree ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶æ by default. ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶ø ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á Degree ‡¶ï‡¶Æ ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßã‡•§

Example: `background-image: linear-gradient(180deg, red, yellow);`

Output Screenshot:

![180deg](./chapter-21-css-gradients/images/180deg.png)

### Direction - 90deg

Example: `background-image: linear-gradient(90deg, red, yellow);`

Output Screenshot:

![](./chapter-21-css-gradients/images/90deg.png)

### Direction - 0% x% 100%

Example: `background-image: linear-gradient(#feffff 0%, #ddf1f9 35%, #a0d8ef 100%);`

![Percentage 1](./chapter-21-css-gradients/images/percentage1.png)

### Direction - 20% 70%

**Example: `background-image: linear-gradient(red 20%, yellow 70%);` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã Position 20% ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá Position 70% ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ Red ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá Yellow Color ‡¶è Transition ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç 0 ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá 20% Solid Red ‡¶ì 70% ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá 100% Solid Yellow Color ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Position ‡¶ì Percentage ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßü‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨ ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ñ‡ßá‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßã, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã Tutorial Online ‡¶è ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§**

Output Screenshot:

![Percentage 1](./chapter-21-css-gradients/images/percentage2.png)

### Direction - 50% 50%

Example: `background-image: linear-gradient(to top right, red 50%, yellow 50%);`

‡¶ñ‡ßá‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶®, ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá 0% ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá 50% ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ Solid red color ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç 50% ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá 100% ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ Solid yellow color ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ Transition ‡¶π‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡¶ó‡¶æ ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶á‡•§

Output Screenshot:

![Percentage 3](./chapter-21-css-gradients/images/percentage3.png)

### Direction - 20% 20%-80% 80%

### Using Transparency as Direction

‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∏‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Color ‡¶á ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ Value ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶¶‡¶Æ ‡ß¶ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶§‡ßá ‡ßß‡ß¶‡ß¶% ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ rgba() function ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø, ‡¶è‡¶á Function ‡¶è‡¶∞ Last Parameter ‡¶è 0 ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá Full Transparency, 1 ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá Full Color (No Transparency).

Example: `background-image: linear-gradient(to right, rgba(255,0,0,0), rgba(255,0,0,1));`

Output Screenshot:

![Transparency](./chapter-21-css-gradients/images/transparency.png)

## Radial Gradients

### Basic Concept of Radial Gradients

- Linear Gradient ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶á Radial Gradient ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶§ ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶æ Colors ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶® ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ Radient Gradient Center ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
- By default, Radiant Gradient ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡ßÉ‡¶§‡¶ø Elipse ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã‡•§
- By default, shape is ellipse, size is farthest-corner, and position is center.
- Radial Gradient - Evenly Spaced Color Stops (this is default).

### By Default Shape of Radial Gradients

Example Code:

```css
background-image: radial-gradient(red, yellow, green);
```

Screenshot:

![By default Radial Gradient](./chapter-21-css-gradients/images/by-deafult.png)

### Circle Shaped Example of Radial Gradients

```css
background-image: radial-gradient(circle, red, yellow, green);
```

Screenshot:

![circle shape](./chapter-21-css-gradients/images/circle.png)

### Providing The % To Tell Where The Color Should Transition

‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Color ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá Transition ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡•§
‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®,

Screenshot:

```css
background-image: radial-gradient(red 5%, yellow 15%, green 60%);
```

**‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá Red 5% ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Yellow 15% ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã 5% ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá 15% ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ Red ‡¶ß‡ßÄ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ß‡ßÄ‡¶∞‡ßá Yellow ‡¶§‡ßá Transition ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ Yellow 15% ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Green 60% ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã, Yellow 15% ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá 60% ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ Yellow ‡¶ß‡ßÄ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ß‡ßÄ‡¶∞‡ßá Green ‡¶è Transition ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶≤‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£‡ßÄ‡ßü ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã, 0-5% ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ Solid Red Color ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç 60%-100% ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ Solid Green Color ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßü‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶ì, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶® Online ‡¶è ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ Tutorial ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶®‡¶ø‡•§**

Screenshot:

![Percentage Again](./chapter-21-css-gradients/images/percentage-again.png)

### Bangladesh Flag Using Radial Gradients

```css
background-image: radial-gradient(circle, red 30%, green 30%);
```

Screenshot:

![Bangladesh Flag](./chapter-21-css-gradients/images/bangladesh-flag.png)

### Position of Radial Gradients

By default, Radiant Gradient ‡¶è‡¶∞ Position `center center` ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á Position ‡¶ï‡ßá Change ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§

Example (Top Center):

```css
background-image: radial-gradient(at top center, red, yellow, green);
```

Screenshot:

![Top Center](./chapter-21-css-gradients/images/top-center.png)

Example: (Right Bottom)

```
background-image: radial-gradient(at right bottom, red, yellow, green);
```

Screenshot:

![right bottom](./chapter-21-css-gradients/images/right-bottom.png)

### Position at X% Y%

‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá `center center` ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶¶‡¶≤‡ßá `50% 50%` ‡¶ì ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø, ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã Center ‡¶ü‡¶æ Left ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá 50% ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Top ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá 50%. ‡¶Ü‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ `right bottom` ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶¶‡¶≤‡ßá `100% 100%` ‡¶ì ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé Center ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® Left ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá 100%, Top ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá 100% Position ‡¶è ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá.
‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ 0%, 50% ‡¶ì 100% ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶Æ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡¶ø Center ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá Left ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá 30% ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Top ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá 40% ‡¶è ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßã ‡¶®‡¶æ, ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø % ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßã‡•§

Example:

```css
background-image: radial-gradient(at 30% 40%, red, yellow, green);
```

Screenshot:

![thirty](./chapter-21-css-gradients/images/thirty.png)

### Position at Closest Side

By default, Radial Gradiant ‡¶è ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Center ‡¶è‡¶∞ Position ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶®, ‡¶∏‡ßá Farthest Corner ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ Transition ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á, Gradient ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® Position ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ Closest Sides ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ Transition ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§

Example:

```css
background-image: radial-gradient(closest-side at 30% 40%, red, yellow, green);
```

Screenshot:

![closest side](./chapter-21-css-gradients/images/closest.png)

### Position at Farthest Side

‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡ßá Position Set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶¨‡ßã, ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá Fartest Side ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ Transition ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

Example:

```css
background-image: radial-gradient(farthest-side at 30% 40%, red, yellow, green);
```

Screenshot:

![Farthest Side](./chapter-21-css-gradients/images/farthest-side.png)

### Position at Closest Corner

‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡ßá Position Set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶¨‡ßã, ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá Closest Corner ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ Transition ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

```css

  closest-corner at 30% 40%,
  red,
  yellow,
  green
```
